openings</span></button></a></div></div></div><div class="layoutPresenters__OuterMargin-sc-30360ab9-1 DiversityAndInclusion__Container-sc-9df2a10f-2 ddTvL dJlloc"><h2 walks together.
    You see the same things. You feel the same feels. You walk out changed for the better.
    We strive to bring that same feeling of connectedness into our workplace. Help us help
    the world experience more live.</p><p class="DiversityAndInclusion__DiversityBody-sc-9df2a10f-1 WTtDF"><a href="/diversity-equity-inclusion">Learn more about diversity, equity &amp; inclusion at SeatGeek</a></p></div><div class="Fans__FansContainer-sc-7a7779e7-0 csQDk"><img src="https://www.seatgeek.com/images/image_uploads/40c16ac9-c64b-4227-acda-f5b665fda4ca/fans.jpeg" class="Fans__FansImage-sc-7a7779e7-1 iqVrkc"/></div><a><button class="Button__ButtonContainer-sc-5deaac4-1 jIZSZu SecondaryButton__StyledSecondaryButton-sc-928b5e3c-0 bosbwx ScrollingViewOpeningsButton__StyledButton-sc-6dce98a0-0 jACeYh"><span class="Button__ButtonContents-sc-5deaac4-2 iNFrxV">View openings</span></button></a><div class="JobsPage__MainContent-sc-d0150daa-3 dqMpON"><div class="JobsPage__CoreValuesMargin-sc-d0150daa-4 iDqPWA"></div><div class="layoutPresenters__OuterMargin-sc-30360ab9-1 ddTvL"><h3 class="TextGrid__GridHeader-sc-39f782c9-0 prvAc">Our core values</h3><div class="TextGrid__GridContainer-sc-39f782c9-2 dwUbvo"><div class="TextElements__TextElementContainer-sc-7146a698-0 gaRqsV"><p class="TextElements__Label-sc-7146a698-4 LwZHi">Start with fans</p><div class="TextElements__BodyContainer-sc-7146a698-2 huryIo"><p class="TextElements__Body-sc-7146a698-5 dJoTlO">When fans win, everyone winsand for too long fans have lost. We challenge ourselves, our partners and our industry to start with fans, and let everything else follow from there.</p></div></div><div class="TextElements__TextElementContainer-sc-7146a698-0 gaRqsV"><p class="TextElements__Label-sc-7146a698-4 LwZHi">Be humbold</p><div class="TextElements__BodyContainer-sc-7146a698-2 huryIo"><p class="TextElements__Body-sc-7146a698-5 dJoTlO">We&#x27;re bold, but humble. We believe we can come up with better ways of doing things through fresher thinking, without being jerks in the process. We&#x27;re brave enough both to go all-in and also to admit when we&#x27;re wrong.</p></div></div><div class="TextElements__TextElementContainer-sc-7146a698-0 gaRqsV"><p class="TextElements__Label-sc-7146a698-4 LwZHi">Pull back the curtains</p><div class="TextElements__BodyContainer-sc-7146a698-2 huryIo"><p class="TextElements__Body-sc-7146a698-5 dJoTlO">We put outsized focus on building the most talented team possible. Exceptional people enabled with context do incredible work, so even when it&#x27;s uncomfortable, we&#x27;re over-the-top transparent with information.</p></div></div><div class="TextElements__TextElementContainer-sc-7146a698-0 gaRqsV"><p class="TextElements__Label-sc-7146a698-4 LwZHi">Don&#x27;t do bullsh*t work</p><div class="TextElements__BodyContainer-sc-7146a698-2 huryIo"><p class="TextElements__Body-sc-7146a698-5 dJoTlO">If unchecked, every job results in too many hours spent on bullsh*t work. We design how we work to spend the most time doing rather than preparing to do. Speed compounds; the fastest to innovate, win.</p></div></div><div class="TextElements__TextElementContainer-sc-7146a698-0 gaRqsV"><p class="TextElements__Label-sc-7146a698-4 LwZHi">Stack the lineup</p><div class="TextElements__BodyContainer-sc-7146a698-2 huryIo"><p class="TextElements__Body-sc-7146a698-5 dJoTlO">Our team is our biggest unfair advantage, and the best teams bring together different backgrounds and experiences. We attract exceptional people who are as diverse as the events we ticket, and strive to create an environment where everyone belongs and maximizes their potential.</p></div></div><div class="TextElements__TextElementContainer-sc-7146a698-0 gaRqsV"><p class="TextElements__Label-sc-7146a698-4 LwZHi">Play long ball</p><div class="TextElements__BodyContainer-sc-7146a698-2 huryIo"><p class="TextElements__Body-sc-7146a698-5 dJoTlO">We take big bets on the future. Often we won&#x27;t know if those bets are successful for months, or even years. Some will fail. Betting on the future means we aren&#x27;t wholly focused on success today. We&#x27;re willing to take those risks because they enable the outsized payoffs that change how fans experience live entertainment.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="OfficeCarousel__CarouselContainer-sc-f62d5a32-0 hBDaUG"><div class="OfficeCarousel__FixedWidthContainer-sc-f62d5a32-1 jNVQAa"><span data-no-ssr="true" class="NoSSR__DefaultOnSSR-sc-4615f9f9-0 cKnFEQ"></span></div></div></div><div class="layoutPresenters__OuterMargin-sc-30360ab9-1 JobsPage__PerksAndBenefitsMargin-sc-d0150daa-5 ddTvL chsAGt"></div><div class="layoutPresenters__OuterMargin-sc-30360ab9-1 ddTvL"><h3 class="TextGrid__GridHeader-sc-39f782c9-0 prvAc">Our perks &amp; benefits</h3><div class="TextGrid__GridContainer-sc-39f782c9-2 dwUbvo"><div class="TextElements__TextElementContainer-sc-7146a698-0 gaRqsV"><p class="TextElements__Label-sc-7146a698-4 LwZHi">Benefits</p><div class="TextElements__BodyContainer-sc-7146a698-2 huryIo"><p class="TextElements__Body-sc-7146a698-5 dJoTlO">We provide access to high-quality health insurance coverage, ample paid time off, and a matching 401k program.</p></div></div><div class="TextElements__TextElementContainer-sc-7146a698-0 gaRqsV"><p class="TextElements__Label-sc-7146a698-4 LwZHi">Parental leave</p><div class="TextElements__BodyContainer-sc-7146a698-2 huryIo"><p class="TextElements__Body-sc-7146a698-5 dJoTlO">Congrats on welcoming a bundle of joy into your life! We offer 16 weeks of leave in a 12-month period.</p></div></div><div class="TextElements__TextElementContainer-sc-7146a698-0 gaRqsV"><p class="TextElements__Label-sc-7146a698-4 LwZHi">Subscriptions</p><div class="TextElements__BodyContainer-sc-7146a698-2 huryIo"><p class="TextElements__Body-sc-7146a698-5 dJoTlO">Health and wellness are incredibly important so we cover employee subscriptions
    to services like One Medical, Ginger.io and Headspace.</p></div></div><div class="TextElements__TextElementContainer-sc-7146a698-0 gaRqsV"><p class="TextElements__Label-sc-7146a698-4 LwZHi">Team events</p><div class="TextElements__BodyContainer-sc-7146a698-2 huryIo"><p class="TextElements__Body-sc-7146a698-5 dJoTlO">Regular virtual team hangs &amp; happy hours are essential, especially while were
    all working remotely. We also put our typical day-to-day work aside for company-wide
    hackathons 3-4 times per year.</p></div></div><div class="TextElements__TextElementContainer-sc-7146a698-0 gaRqsV"><p class="TextElements__Label-sc-7146a698-4 LwZHi">Ticket perk</p><div class="TextElements__BodyContainer-sc-7146a698-2 huryIo"><p class="TextElements__Body-sc-7146a698-5 dJoTlO">SeatGeek employees receive a monthly ticket-purchase stipend for live events!</p></div></div><div class="TextElements__TextElementContainer-sc-7146a698-0 gaRqsV"><p class="TextElements__Label-sc-7146a698-4 LwZHi">Flexible work environment</p><div class="TextElements__BodyContainer-sc-7146a698-2 huryIo"><p class="TextElements__Body-sc-7146a698-5 dJoTlO">Flexible work environment, allowing you to work as many days a week in the office as youd like or 100% remotely.  A WFH stipend to support your home office setup.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="Carousel__Section-sc-c7782698-3 cKwnxS"><div class="layoutPresenters__OuterMargin-sc-30360ab9-1
